        "from unsloth import FastLanguageModel\n",
        "import torch\n",
        "max_seq_length = 2048 # Choose any! We auto support RoPE Scaling internally!\n",
        "dtype = None # None for auto detection. Float16 for Tesla T4, V100, Bfloat16 for Ampere+\n",
        "load_in_4bit = True # Use 4bit quantization to reduce memory usage. Can be False.\n",
        "\n",
        "# 4bit pre quantized models we support for 4x faster downloading + no OOMs.\n",
        "fourbit_models = [\n",
        "    \"unsloth/Meta-Llama-3.1-8B-bnb-4bit\",      # Llama-3.1 15 trillion tokens model 2x faster!\n",
        "    \"unsloth/Meta-Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct-bnb-4bit\",\n",

        "    model_name = \"unsloth/Llama-3.2-3B-Instruct\",\n",

        "    dtype = dtype,\n",
        "    load_in_4bit = load_in_4bit,\n",
        "    # token = \"hf_...\", # use one if using gated models like meta-llama/Llama-2-7b-hf\n",

        "    target_modules = [\"q_proj\", \"k_proj\", \"v_proj\", \"o_proj\",\n",
        "                      \"gate_proj\", \"up_proj\", \"down_proj\",],\n",
        "    lora_alpha = 16,\n",
        "    lora_dropout = 0, # Supports any, but = 0 is optimized\n",

        "    use_gradient_checkpointing = \"unsloth\", # True or \"unsloth\" for very long context\n",

      "cell_type": "code",
      "source": [
        "import os\n",
        "import json\n",
        "import random\n",
        "import time\n",
        "import re\n",
        "from tqdm import tqdm\n",
        "from google import genai\n",
        "from google.genai import types\n",
        "\n",
        "api_key=os.environ.get(\"AIzaSyDQPHg4CdFiqhtMcxjdhenXji88Re2YbPk\")\n",
        "client = genai.Client(\n",
        "    api_key=\"AIzaSyDQPHg4CdFiqhtMcxjdhenXji88Re2YbPk\"\n",
        ")\n",
        "MODEL = \"gemini-2.0-flash\"\n",
        "\n",
        "def stream_response(prompt, temperature=0.7, retries=5):\n",
        "    \"\"\"Safely get streamed response from Gemini with retry on 429\"\"\"\n",
        "    delay = 10  # initial delay between retries in seconds\n",
        "    for attempt in range(retries):\n",
        "        try:\n",
        "            chunks = client.models.generate_content_stream(\n",
        "                model=MODEL,\n",
        "                contents=prompt,\n",
        "                config=types.GenerateContentConfig(\n",
        "                    response_mime_type=\"text/plain\",\n",
        "                    temperature=temperature,\n",
        "                    max_output_tokens=1000,\n",
        "                )\n",
        "            )\n",
        "            return ''.join(chunk.text for chunk in chunks if chunk.text)\n",
        "        except Exception as e:\n",
        "            err_msg = str(e)\n",
        "            print(f\"Attempt {attempt + 1}: Gemini Error: {err_msg}\")\n",
        "\n",
        "            # Retry logic for quota errors\n",
        "            if \"RESOURCE_EXHAUSTED\" in err_msg or \"429\" in err_msg:\n",
        "                match = re.search(r'retryDelay.*?(\\d+)s', err_msg)\n",
        "                wait_time = int(match.group(1)) if match else delay\n",
        "                print(f\"üïí Waiting {wait_time} seconds before retrying...\")\n",
        "                time.sleep(wait_time)\n",
        "            else:\n",
        "                break\n",
        "    return None\n",
        "\n",
        "def generate_illness_list():\n",
        "    \"\"\"Get a list of common illnesses\"\"\"\n",
        "    prompt = \"\"\"\n",
        "List 100 common illnesses or minor health problems people often treat with home remedies. Focus on general or everyday issues like \"cold\", \"headache\", \"cough\", \"indigestion\", etc.\n",
        "\n",
        "Return a Python list of strings only.\n",
        "\"\"\"\n",
        "    response = stream_response(prompt, temperature=0.4)\n",
        "    try:\n",
        "        return list(set(eval(response)))  # ensure uniqueness\n",
        "    except:\n",
        "        return [\"cold\", \"headache\", \"sore throat\", \"indigestion\", \"nausea\", \"constipation\", \"dry cough\"]\n",
        "\n",
        "def generate_remedy(illness):\n",
        "    \"\"\"Generate a home remedy for a given illness\"\"\"\n",
        "    prompt = f\"\"\"\n",
        "You are a home remedy expert. Provide a helpful, safe, and natural home remedy for the following condition:\n",
        "\n",
        "Illness: \"{illness}\"\n",
        "\n",
        "Use household ingredients (like honey, ginger, turmeric, salt water, etc). Do NOT mention prescription drugs. Keep it under 80 words. Return only the remedy text, no bullet points or explanations.\n",
        "\"\"\"\n",
        "    return stream_response(prompt, temperature=0.8)\n",
        "\n",
        "def create_remedy_dataset(num_samples=1000):\n",
        "    print(\"Generating illness list...\")\n",
        "    illnesses = generate_illness_list()\n",
        "    print(f\"Got {len(illnesses)} base illnesses.\")\n",
        "\n",
        "    dataset = set()\n",
        "    examples = []\n",
        "\n",
        "    print(\"Generating remedies...\")\n",
        "    with tqdm(total=num_samples) as pbar:\n",
        "        while len(examples) < num_samples:\n",
        "            illness = random.choice(illnesses)\n",
        "            remedy = generate_remedy(illness)\n",
        "\n",
        "            if not remedy:\n",
        "                continue\n",
        "\n",
        "            key = (illness.strip().lower(), remedy.strip().lower())\n",
        "            if key in dataset:\n",
        "                continue\n",
        "\n",
        "            dataset.add(key)\n",
        "            examples.append({\n",
        "                \"instruction\": \"Suggest a natural home remedy for the illness.\",\n",
        "                \"input\": f\"Illness: {illness}\",\n",
        "                \"output\": remedy.strip()\n",
        "            })\n",
        "            pbar.update(1)\n",
        "            time.sleep(1)  # Avoid hitting rate limits\n",
        "\n",
        "    with open(\"home_remedies_dataset.jsonl\", \"w\") as f:\n",
        "        for item in examples:\n",
        "            f.write(json.dumps(item) + \"\\n\")\n",
        "\n",
        "    print(f\"\\n‚úÖ Finished: {len(examples)} unique examples generated.\")\n",
        "\n",
        "if __name__ == \"__main__\":\n",
        "    create_remedy_dataset()\n"

        "We now use the Alpaca dataset from [yahma](https://huggingface.co/datasets/yahma/alpaca-cleaned), which is a filtered version of 52K of the original [Alpaca dataset](https://crfm.stanford.edu/2023/03/13/alpaca.html). You can replace this code section with your own data prep.\n",
        "\n",
        "**[NOTE]** To train only on completions (ignoring the user's input) read TRL's docs [here](https://huggingface.co/docs/trl/sft_trainer#train-on-completions-only).\n",
        "\n",
        "**[NOTE]** Remember to add the **EOS_TOKEN** to the tokenized output!! Otherwise you'll get infinite generations!\n",

        "\n",

        "from datasets import load_dataset\n",
        "alpaca_prompt = \"\"\"Below is an instruction that describes a task, paired with an input that provides further context. Write a response that appropriately completes the request.\n",
        "\n",
        "### Instruction:\n",
        "{}\n",
        "\n",
        "### Input:\n",
        "{}\n",
        "\n",
        "### Response:\n",
        "{}\"\"\"\n",
        "\n",
        "EOS_TOKEN = tokenizer.eos_token # Must add EOS_TOKEN\n",
        "def formatting_prompts_func(examples):\n",
        "    instructions = examples[\"instruction\"]\n",
        "    inputs       = examples[\"input\"]\n",
        "    outputs      = examples[\"output\"]\n",
        "    texts = []\n",
        "    for instruction, input, output in zip(instructions, inputs, outputs):\n",
        "        # Must add EOS_TOKEN, otherwise your generation will go on forever!\n",
        "        text = alpaca_prompt.format(instruction, input, output) + EOS_TOKEN\n",
        "        texts.append(text)\n",
        "    return { \"text\" : texts, }\n",
        "pass\n",
        "\n",
        "#from datasets import load_dataset\n",

        "    tokenizer = tokenizer,\n",
        "    train_dataset = dataset,\n",
        "    dataset_text_field = \"text\",\n",
        "    max_seq_length = max_seq_length,\n",
        "    dataset_num_proc = 2,\n",
        "    packing = False, # Can make training 5x faster for short sequences.\n",
        "    args = TrainingArguments(\n",
        "        per_device_train_batch_size = 2,\n",
        "        gradient_accumulation_steps = 4,\n",

        "        bf16 = is_bfloat16_supported(),\n",
        "        logging_steps = 1,\n",
        "        optim = \"adamw_8bit\",\n",
        "        weight_decay = 0.01,\n",
        "        lr_scheduler_type = \"linear\",\n",
        "        seed = 3407,\n",
        "        output_dir = \"outputs\",\n",

      "source": [
        "# Home remedies prompt generation using Alpaca format\n",
        "from transformers import TextStreamer\n",
        "\n",
        "# Illness to generate a remedy for\n",
        "illness = \"Sore throat\"\n",
        "\n",
        "# Alpaca-style prompt template\n",
        "alpaca_prompt = (\n",
        "    \"Below is an instruction that describes a task, paired with an input that provides further context. \"\n",
        "    \"Write a response that appropriately completes the request.\\n\\n\"\n",
        "    \"### Instruction:\\n{}\\n\\n### Input:\\n{}\\n\\n### Response:\\n{}\"\n",
        ")\n",
        "\n",
        "# Create the input tensor\n",
        "inputs = tokenizer(\n",
        "    [\n",
        "        alpaca_prompt.format(\n",
        "            \"You are a home remedy expert. Suggest a safe, natural remedy using common household ingredients. Keep it under 80 words. Do NOT recommend prescription drugs.\",  # instruction\n",
        "            f\"Illness: {illness}\",  # input\n",
        "            \"\"  # output left blank for generation\n",
        "        )\n",
        "    ],\n",
        "    return_tensors=\"pt\"\n",
        ").to(\"cuda\")\n",
        "\n",
        "# Enable fast inference (if supported)\n",
        "FastLanguageModel.for_inference(model)\n",
        "\n",
        "# Stream the generated remedy\n",
        "text_streamer = TextStreamer(tokenizer)\n",
        "_ = model.generate(**inputs, streamer=text_streamer, max_new_tokens=80)\n"
      ]
    },

        "id": "TCv4vXHd61i7"
      },
      "source": [
        "### GGUF / llama.cpp Conversion\n",
        "To save to `GGUF` / `llama.cpp`, we support it natively now! We clone `llama.cpp` and we default save it to `q8_0`. We allow all methods like `q4_k_m`. Use `save_pretrained_gguf` for local saving and `push_to_hub_gguf` for uploading to HF.\n",
        "\n",
        "Some supported quant methods (full list on our [Wiki page](https://github.com/unslothai/unsloth/wiki#gguf-quantization-options)):\n",
        "* `q8_0` - Fast conversion. High resource use, but generally acceptable.\n",
        "* `q4_k_m` - Recommended. Uses Q6_K for half of the attention.wv and feed_forward.w2 tensors, else Q4_K.\n",
        "* `q5_k_m` - Recommended. Uses Q6_K for half of the attention.wv and feed_forward.w2 tensors, else Q5_K.\n",
        "\n"
      ]

      "cell_type": "code",
      "source": [
        "import gradio as gr\n",
        "from unsloth import FastLanguageModel\n",
        "from transformers import TextStreamer\n",
        "import torch\n",
        "import socket\n",
        "import os\n",
        "import threading\n",
        "from queue import Queue\n",
        "\n",
        "# --- Configuration ---\n",
        "MODEL_NAME = \"jagruthh/home_remedies_model\"\n",
        "MAX_SEQ_LENGTH = 2048\n",
        "LOAD_IN_4BIT = True\n",
        "\n",
        "# Global variables\n",
        "model = None\n",
        "tokenizer = None\n",
        "\n",
        "def find_available_port(start_port=7860, max_attempts=20):\n",
        "    for port in range(start_port, start_port + max_attempts):\n",
        "        try:\n",
        "            with socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM) as s:\n",
        "                s.bind(('', port))\n",
        "                return port\n",
        "        except OSError:\n",
        "            continue\n",
        "    raise OSError(\"No available ports found.\")\n",
        "\n",
        "def load_model_and_tokenizer():\n",
        "    global model, tokenizer\n",
        "    if model is None or tokenizer is None:\n",
        "        print(f\"Loading model: {MODEL_NAME}...\")\n",
        "        model, tokenizer = FastLanguageModel.from_pretrained(\n",
        "            model_name=MODEL_NAME,\n",
        "            max_seq_length=MAX_SEQ_LENGTH,\n",
        "            dtype=None,\n",
        "            load_in_4bit=LOAD_IN_4BIT,\n",
        "        )\n",
        "        FastLanguageModel.for_inference(model)\n",
        "        if tokenizer.pad_token is None:\n",
        "            tokenizer.pad_token = tokenizer.eos_token\n",
        "    return model, tokenizer\n",
        "\n",
        "class GradioTextStreamer(TextStreamer):\n",
        "    def __init__(self, tokenizer, queue: Queue, skip_prompt: bool = True, **decode_kwargs):\n",
        "        super().__init__(tokenizer, skip_prompt=skip_prompt, **decode_kwargs)\n",
        "        self.queue = queue\n",
        "        self.stop_signal = None\n",
        "        self.timeout = 120\n",
        "\n",
        "    def on_finalized_text(self, text: str, stream_end: bool = False):\n",
        "        self.queue.put(text, timeout=self.timeout)\n",
        "        if stream_end:\n",
        "            self.queue.put(self.stop_signal, timeout=self.timeout)\n",
        "\n",
        "# --- Prompt ---\n",
        "REMEDY_INSTRUCTION = (\n",
        "    \"You are a home remedy expert. Suggest a safe, natural remedy using common household ingredients \"\n",
        "    \"like honey, ginger, turmeric, etc. Do NOT suggest prescription medication. Keep your response under 80 words.\"\n",
        ")\n",
        "\n",
        "@torch.inference_mode()\n",
        "def generate_remedy(illness):\n",
        "    global model, tokenizer\n",
        "    if model is None or tokenizer is None:\n",
        "        load_model_and_tokenizer()\n",
        "        if model is None or tokenizer is None:\n",
        "            yield \"Error: Model not loaded.\"\n",
        "            return\n",
        "\n",
        "    input_text = f\"Illness: {illness}\"\n",
        "    prompt = f\"\"\"Below is an instruction that describes a task, paired with an input that provides further context. Write a response that appropriately completes the request.\n",
        "\n",
        "### Instruction:\n",
        "{REMEDY_INSTRUCTION}\n",
        "\n",
        "### Input:\n",
        "{input_text}\n",
        "\n",
        "### Response:\n",
        "\"\"\"\n",
        "\n",
        "    inputs = tokenizer([prompt], return_tensors=\"pt\").to(\"cuda\")\n",
        "    q = Queue()\n",
        "    streamer = GradioTextStreamer(tokenizer, q, skip_prompt=True)\n",
        "\n",
        "    def generation_thread_func():\n",
        "        try:\n",
        "            model.generate(\n",
        "                inputs=inputs[\"input_ids\"],\n",
        "                attention_mask=inputs[\"attention_mask\"],\n",
        "                streamer=streamer,\n",
        "                max_new_tokens=200,\n",
        "                temperature=0.7,\n",
        "                top_p=0.9,\n",
        "                do_sample=True,\n",
        "                pad_token_id=tokenizer.pad_token_id,\n",
        "                eos_token_id=tokenizer.eos_token_id\n",
        "            )\n",
        "        except Exception as e:\n",
        "            q.put(f\"\\n\\nGeneration Error: {e}\")\n",
        "            q.put(None)\n",
        "\n",
        "    thread = threading.Thread(target=generation_thread_func)\n",
        "    thread.start()\n",
        "\n",
        "    generated_text = \"\"\n",
        "    while True:\n",
        "        try:\n",
        "            next_token = q.get(timeout=120)\n",
        "            if next_token is streamer.stop_signal:\n",
        "                break\n",
        "            generated_text += next_token\n",
        "            # Strip known EOS tokens if they appear mid-stream\n",
        "            clean_text = generated_text.strip().replace(\"<|eot_id|>\", \"\").replace(\"</s>\", \"\").strip()  # CHANGE\n",
        "            yield clean_text\n",
        "        except Queue.empty:\n",
        "            if not thread.is_alive():\n",
        "                break\n",
        "            continue\n",
        "        except Exception as e:\n",
        "            print(f\"Error reading from queue: {e}\")\n",
        "            break\n",
        "\n",
        "    thread.join(timeout=5)\n",
        "\n",
        "# Load model before UI\n",
        "load_model_and_tokenizer()\n",
        "\n",
        "# Illness examples\n",
        "examples = [\n",
        "    [\"headache\"],\n",
        "    [\"cough\"],\n",
        "    [\"indigestion\"],\n",
        "    [\"sore throat\"],\n",
        "    [\"constipation\"],\n",
        "    [\"nausea\"],\n",
        "    [\"sunburn\"],\n",
        "    [\"muscle cramps\"],\n",
        "]\n",
        "\n",
        "# CSS for UI\n",
        "css = \"\"\"\n",
        "    .gradio-container { font-family: 'Segoe UI', sans-serif; }\n",
        "    .feedback-box textarea {\n",
        "        background-color: #fefcf9; /* soft cream background */  /* CHANGE */\n",
        "        border: 1px solid #ddd;\n",
        "        padding: 12px;\n",
        "        border-radius: 10px;\n",
        "        color: #2e2e2e;  /* CHANGE */\n",
        "        font-size: 16px;\n",
        "    }\n",
        "    .title {\n",
        "        font-size: 32px;\n",
        "        color: #2f855a;\n",
        "        font-weight: bold;\n",
        "        text-align: center;\n",
        "        margin-bottom: 20px;\n",
        "    }\n",
        "    .section-title {\n",
        "        font-size: 20px;\n",
        "        margin-bottom: 10px;\n",
        "        color: #4a5568;\n",
        "        font-weight: 600;\n",
        "    }\n",
        "    .gr-button-primary {\n",
        "        background-color: #38a169 !important;\n",
        "        color: white !important;\n",
        "    }\n",
        "\"\"\"\n",
        "\n",
        "# --- Gradio UI ---\n",
        "with gr.Blocks(theme=gr.themes.Soft(), css=css) as demo:\n",
        "    gr.Markdown(\"<div class='title'>üåø Natural Home Remedies Generator</div>\")\n",
        "\n",
        "    with gr.Row():\n",
        "        with gr.Column(scale=1):\n",
        "            gr.Markdown(\"<div class='section-title'>ü©∫ What‚Äôs the illness?</div>\")\n",
        "            illness_input = gr.Textbox(\n",
        "                placeholder=\"e.g., headache, sore throat, indigestion...\",\n",
        "                lines=2,\n",
        "                show_label=False\n",
        "            )\n",
        "            submit_btn = gr.Button(\"üåº Suggest Remedy\", variant=\"primary\")\n",
        "            gr.Markdown(\"<hr><div class='section-title'>üß™ Try these:</div>\")\n",
        "            gr.Examples(\n",
        "                examples=examples,\n",
        "                inputs=[illness_input],\n",
        "                label=\"Sample Illnesses\",\n",
        "            )\n",
        "\n",
        "        with gr.Column(scale=2):\n",
        "            gr.Markdown(\"<div class='section-title'>üí° Home Remedy</div>\")\n",
        "            remedy_output = gr.Textbox(\n",
        "                label=None,\n",
        "                interactive=False,\n",
        "                lines=8,\n",
        "                elem_classes=\"feedback-box\"\n",
        "            )\n",
        "\n",
        "    submit_btn.click(\n",
        "        fn=generate_remedy,\n",
        "        inputs=[illness_input],\n",
        "        outputs=remedy_output,\n",
        "        api_name=\"remedy\"\n",
        "    )\n",
        "\n",
        "# --- Launch ---\n",
        "if __name__ == \"__main__\":\n",
        "    try:\n",
        "        port = find_available_port()\n",
        "        print(f\"‚úÖ Launching on port: {port}\")\n",
        "        demo.launch(\n",
        "            server_name=\"0.0.0.0\",\n",
        "            server_port=port,\n",
        "            share=True\n",
        "        )\n",
        "    except Exception as e:\n",
        "        print(f\"‚ùå Error launching app: {e}\")\n"
      ],
